Special Telecommunications Issue

Important Statistics of Telecommunications in the Past Four Years 174

— Zhen

——From the Fourth National Congress to the Fifth National Congress——

The Fifth National Congress concluded on the 23rd of last month. With different ideas gathered together, and national policies decided through public discussions, to review the past and encourage the future, uniting with sincerity to save the nation, this is truly a grand event. I have read the Congress's declaration, which is plain and unadorned, with words filled with sorrow, pointing out the areas that require effort in the future, striking at the heart of current problems. The second item of the fourth section is to develop transportation to enrich the economy. Transportation is the lifeline of a country, and telecommunications is its nervous system. If the lifeline stops moving, it loses its vitality; if the nervous system is not functioning well, it loses its sense of awareness. Loss of awareness is no different from being lifeless. Therefore, the nervous system is the source of human thought, and the telecommunications system is the hub of national administration. In recent years, the Ministry of Transportation has made improvements to the postal and telecommunications industries. The various facts have been published in this journal, and there is no need to repeat them. However, from the Fourth National Congress to the Fifth National Congress, four years have passed. What are the achievements in telecommunications construction and reorganization? It is necessary to use concise statistical figures to illustrate it, for comparison and learning.

Based on the tables above, except for personnel and debt, there has been a considerable increase in everything else. In other words, consumption costs have been reduced as much as possible, while the scope of business has increased in various ways. Although the telecommunications industry is state-owned, it has not been subsidized by the national treasury. It is entirely operated by "using electricity to support electricity" and "using electricity to build electricity," starting with itself. Each year, about five million in telecommunications fees owed by government troops cannot be collected. Since the outbreak of national disasters, natural and man-made disasters have been pressing. Rural areas have gone bankrupt, markets have shrunk, and telecommunications business has been affected. Therefore, the telecommunications economy is extremely difficult in this environment! Although there are various plans, they cannot be realized as scheduled. However, the telecommunications authorities have overcome all difficulties with hard work and determination and have made rapid progress. Over the years, they have established a foundation and gained social sympathy. If they can maintain this spirit and redouble their efforts, there will be even more hopeful results at the Sixth National Congress.

The Characteristics of the New Telegraph Code Published by the Ministry of Transportation 175

— Qinghua

Before 1929, the "New Telegraph Code" was only sold by private publishers. The content was very simple, and errors were unavoidable. Moreover, the "New Telegraph Code" sold by private publishers was only for profit. The paper was brittle and not durable, the printing was poor and harmful to the eyes, and the various telegraph regulations attached were often full of errors, either abolished or revised and supplemented, which could cause misunderstandings. In view of this, the Ministry of Transportation published a "New Telegraph Code" in October 1929, printed on durable Daolin paper, with accurate telegraph rules and bureau names attached, and the price was very low, only recovering the cost of one jiao per book. After the book was published, it was convenient for society. In August 1933, the Ministry of Transportation reprinted the code because the stock was sold out. The content was greatly improved, and the main points are as follows:

(1) The telegraph code is printed with Arabic numerals. The old telegraph code was printed with Chinese characters, such as "七一九三," which is now changed to "7193," which is exactly the same as the telegraph code written on the incoming and outgoing telegrams, making it more convenient to translate the telegraph code than before.

(2) Enlarging commonly used characters. There are more than 9,000 characters in the "New Telegraph Code," but only two or three thousand characters are commonly used in telegrams. For the convenience of searching, the commonly used characters are printed in large characters to make them conspicuous and easy to find.

(3) Adding stroke counts to characters of the same radical. There are many characters in the same radical, such as the water radical, wood radical, and metal radical. Searching for a character in that radical sometimes takes one or two minutes, which is extremely difficult. For the convenience of searching, the method of dividing strokes in dictionaries is used to add stroke counts under each line, so that after finding the radical, characters can be searched according to the number of strokes, saving time.

(4) Adding a table for easily searching difficult characters. The organization of Chinese characters is complex, and there are quite a few characters with unclear radicals. If only the radical table is used to search for characters, difficulties may still arise. Therefore, the characters with unclear radicals that are difficult to find are arranged in order according to the number of strokes in each character. Whenever encountering a character with a dubious radical, the number of strokes in the character can be calculated and found in this table immediately. The telegraph code is printed in the table at the same time, so when the character is found, the telegraph code is known, and there is no need to check the telegraph code in the main part of the book again.

(5) Adding a four-corner code difficult character lookup table. When encountering a character with an unclear radical, the number of strokes can be calculated and used to search the "Difficult Character Easy Lookup Table," as mentioned in the previous section, but Chinese characters have different forms, such as ancient, formal, cursive, and colloquial. When calculating the number of strokes, it is often because of being accustomed to colloquial or cursive characters that the calculated number is not accurate, so it is still impossible to find it immediately in the table. For example, the character "享" has eight strokes in its formal form and nine strokes in its colloquial form (享). Therefore, to make searching more convenient, the difficult-to-find characters are arranged according to the four-corner code, which can reduce the difficulty!

(6) Necessarily add needed characters (183). In recent years, the scope of telegraph applications has gradually expanded, so there is a great need to add characters. When compiling and printing this time, 183 new characters were added after review, and for the convenience of checking, a "New Added Character Code Reference Table" was specially compiled and attached for reference.

(7) Deleting 46 duplicate characters. There are many duplicate characters in the old version of the "New Telegraph Code." For example, the character "穴" is found in both the 宀 radical and the 穴 radical. The telegraph code in the 宀 radical is 1340, and the telegraph code in the 穴 radical is 4494. In order to avoid duplication and make it easier to remember the telegraph code, 46 duplicate characters with the same character but different codes have been deleted. However, the telegraph codes of the deleted characters will not be replaced temporarily to avoid misunderstandings. A special table is also printed for reference for these deleted duplicate characters.

(8) Using telegraph codes to represent dates and times. The date and time of telegrams were traditionally replaced by rhyme titles and time periods. For example, one day and twelve o'clock is replaced by the two characters "東午". Anyone who is not familiar with the rhyme titles must search the "Rhyme Title Date Replacement Table" once, which is extremely inconvenient. Now, the remaining telegraph codes are used to directly replace the date and time. From 9801 to 9824 represents one to twenty-four o'clock, and 9901 to 9913 represents the first to thirty-first day of the month. The first two codes of 98 replace the telegraph code for time, and 99 replaces the telegraph code for date, which is easy to remember without having to check the table.

(9) Special index of cipher page numbers. When compiling the code of "New Telegraph Code", the thousand and hundred digits of the new code on the corner are often not arranged in sequential order and are reversed. When translating incoming telegrams, it is very difficult to find them. For the convenience of translation, a special page index of cipher is prepared. The table is divided into two lines, one line arranges the first two digits of the cipher in order, and the other line fills in the page number where the cipher is located. The two are compared, and the translation is extremely convenient.

(10) Adding new Roman alphabet telegraph codes. Ordinary telegraph codes consist of four numerals. If sending to foreign countries, each character must be charged at the full price. Roman alphabet telegraph codes consist of three foreign letters. After the entire telegram is translated into this telegraph code, it can be concatenated into an international code of five letters per group, which is calculated at 60% of the full price per character, and the number of characters can be reduced. Each telegram can save 64% of the telegraph fee. It is much cheaper for overseas Chinese to use it to communicate with their motherland.

The above ten points are the characteristics of the improved version of the code. Therefore, sales were very rapid after publication, and it was sold out by the end of last year. The Ministry of Transportation reprinted the code because merchants from various places requested to purchase it and needed it very much. The content was greatly refreshed, and an appendix "Telecommunications Handbook" was added. It was printed in August of this year and has now been published. The content is richer and the printing is more sophisticated. The length is one-third longer than the original. It is said that the cost of each book is 3 jiao of national currency, but the Ministry of Transportation still sells each book for 2 jiao to promote it, because the code has some advertising revenue. In addition to the previous improvements that have been preserved, the code has the following improvements:

(1) Horizontal arrangement of character codes. The character codes of the old version of the "New Telegraph Code" were arranged in vertical lines. However, the telegraph codes use Arabic numerals, and there are Roman alphabet telegraph codes, which are usually arranged horizontally. After the character codes are arranged horizontally, the radicals and stroke counts printed on the side of the book can be compared with each line, which is much more convenient when checking characters. Also, the telegraph codes arranged on each page of the original code, such as the first page from 0001 to 0100, and the second page from 0101 to 0200, when translating incoming telegrams, a code of 0100 is often mistaken for being listed on the second page. When checking the second page, it is only discovered that the code is listed on the first page. In short, the telegraph codes listed on each page must have a telegraph code with a different hundred digit, which does not seem neat. Now it is changed to the first page from 0000 to 0099, and the second page from 0100 to 0199, so that it is completely consistent with the thousand and hundred digit telegraph codes annotated on the corner.

(2) Adding the appendix "Telecommunications Handbook". The unique feature of this newly published "New Telegraph Code" is the addition of the appendix "Telecommunications Handbook", which is very extensive, with a total of one hundred and fifty-five pages. In addition to the telegraph regulations, price lists, bureau names, etc., which are all included in the handbook, the following two items have been newly added:

(1) Chronological Table of Major Telecommunications Events. The Chinese public is very unfamiliar with the past history of domestic telecommunications. Few domestic publications record the past situation of telecommunications. Therefore, a chronological table of major telecommunications events in the past years has been compiled for the public to consult the past traces of telecommunications, which is very valuable.

(2) Description of the Current Status of Telecommunications. The development of China's telecommunications industry has been quite rapid in recent years. It is believed that the general situation is welcome to the Chinese people. Therefore, the current status of telecommunications is summarized and described so that the Chinese people have a general idea of the current status of telecommunications and are not too unfamiliar. A simple diagram of important national wireless communication circuits is attached for reference.

(This newly published "New Telegraph Code" is sold in telegraph bureaus and radio stations in various places, but it may arrive a little later in places farther from the capital. If you want to purchase it urgently, you can write to this newspaper office to purchase it on your behalf. In addition to the actual price of 2 jiao per book, a postage fee of 5 fen should be added, and 8 fen should be added for registration. Postage stamps are fully acceptable.)

The Legal Issue of Broadcasting Gramophone Records by Radio Stations Resolved 176

— Yun

The Shanghai Foreign Gramophone Record Company previously proposed six demands to the Tianhai Wireless Broadcasting Industry Association because the broadcasting of records by various broadcasting radio stations during broadcasting had a huge impact on the gramophone record business. Among the most important demands was that each broadcasting radio station must pay a copyright fee of 150 yuan per day for broadcasting records, to be paid in full on the first day of each month. If the above requirements were rejected, legal action would be taken, and it was said that a similar lawsuit had recently occurred in the UK, and the record company had won. After receiving the report, the Ministry of Transportation believed that broadcasting radio stations were an important tool for promoting public education. In addition to setting up broadcasting stations in Shanghai, Beiping, and other places, all private broadcasting radio stations in the country were under the supervision of the Ministry in accordance with the law. In order to attract listeners, these radio stations must appropriately include entertainment programs in addition to various educational programs to increase interest, and broadcasting records is the most convenient and economical of all entertainment programs. Therefore, the Ministry paid great attention to the above-mentioned requirements of the foreign record company. However, when the foreign company made the above requirements, it said that if it was not done, it would take legal action, because the record was also one of the publications or works, so it should enjoy copyright. If others want to publicly broadcast it, they must first obtain the consent of the author, otherwise it is an infringement of the author's interests. If this is the case, then the prerequisite question of this case is, according to the current copyright law and publication law in our country, can the record be regarded as a work or publication and enjoy copyright? If it can enjoy copyright, must all broadcasting radio stations obtain the consent of the record company to broadcast records by wireless radio? Once these two points are resolved, whether the requirements of the foreign record company are legal can be easily solved.

Although the Ministry of Transportation has studied the above-mentioned problems in detail, it has formally requested the Judicial Yuan to explain it for the sake of caution because it involves the law. Recently, the Judicial Yuan replied to the Ministry of Transportation that the case had been resolved by the Unified Interpretation of Laws and Regulations Conference of the Judicial Yuan:

"Gramophone records are neither publications nor works, and there is no exclusive right to public performance. The purchaser can use it in any way based on their ownership, regardless of whether it is for personal entertainment or for public listening. The seller, manufacturer, and publisher shall not interfere."

According to the Unified Interpretation of Laws and Regulations Conference of the Judicial Yuan, it is the highest authority in the country for interpreting laws. Now that it is so firmly and clearly denying that gramophone records are works or publications and have no exclusive right to public performance, then there is no legal problem with broadcasting records by radio stations.

What Telephone Users are Expected to Do After the Implementation of the Call Inspection System 177

— Zhongming

In order to promote the telephone business, the Ministry of Transportation has designated business inspectors of more than a dozen telegraph bureaus in Shanghai, Tianjin, and other places to serve concurrently as local telephone business inspectors. This method has been implemented since October 1, and two months have passed so far. It is reported that based on the results of inspections in the past two months, the problems of the telephone business in various places can be summarized into two parts: one part occurs on the telephone bureau side, and the other part occurs on the user side. Now I am writing here to talk about it.

The problems that occur on the telephone bureau side are nothing more than: (1) Telephone bureau employees soliciting drinking expenses from users; (2) Lack of courtesy to users; (3) Slow connection by drivers; (4) Slow repair by the telephone bureau when machines are damaged, etc. These things do cause inconvenience and unpleasant feelings for users. However, these events are not what the telephone bureau wants, but only the actions of some irresponsible and disloyal employees. Therefore, the telephone authorities are very willing to thoroughly eliminate them. But before the elimination, we must first ask telephone users to cooperate closely with the telephone bureau. It is heard that when business inspectors in various places ask users whether there are any of the above-mentioned problems, many telephone users are willing to report the facts and ask for investigation; but there are not a few who are evasive and vague in their answers. The general idea of telephone users is to "treat people with kindness" and "make small things nothing," fearing that once reported, the person concerned will inevitably be subject to considerable punishment. But at the same time, they secretly resent the poor telephone business. We are very grateful to those who tell the truth! Because they have given great help to the improvement of the telephone business. As for those who generally feel dissatisfied but still endure and do not reveal the truth, I hope to change their attitude, because the poor telephone business causes great suffering to the users, and the telephone bureau also loses great reputation. If you do not tell the truth and cooperate, the telephone business will never be improved. All undertakings must be worked hard in many ways to be effective. The telephone business also needs to be worked hard in many ways to have full improvement potential. At the same time, I also hope that the public will release the power of sanctions, and don't have the previous misunderstanding and condone evil!

In the past few years, the Ministry of Transportation has been working hard to improve both the telegraph and telephone services. The purpose is nothing more than to seek convenience for the public. This fact should be known to the social people. The establishment of business inspectors, the main purpose is also here, their only task is to seek the contact between telegram and telephone users and the telephone bureau, so as to consult all matters that the public hopes from the telephone bureau, and report to the authorities for adoption and implementation. Therefore, users should thoroughly understand their mission and cooperate with them. If you encounter the above-mentioned problems, please report them at any time, and you will surely receive a satisfactory answer. If the telephone bureau finds that the situation is true, the employees who should be responsible will be punished in accordance with the regulations, and there will be no leniency or perfunctory handling. If you proceed in this way, you can achieve the effect of punishing one to warn a hundred.

As for the problems that occur on the telephone user side, they are nothing more than: (1) The type reported by the user does not match the actual situation; (2) Private installation of extensions, intercoms, or small switchboards; (3) Private relocation of machines, change of name, or transfer of ownership. Here, I do not want to discuss it from a moral or legal point of view, but only want to say something about the impact on the telephone business: First, falsely reporting the type and privately installing machines will reduce the telephone bureau's income and hinder the telephone bureau's economy. Second, private installation of extensions will increase the load on the telephone and shorten the life of the telephone. Third, private relocation of the telephone is easy to block the call, and if you are careless and accidentally touch the electric light line, the user will suffer even more. Fourth, private change of name or transfer of ownership is enough to disrupt the accuracy of telephone exchange and cause criticism from other users. All of this is greatly detrimental to telephone services.

Since the start of telephone business inspection, although it has only been two months, there have been many cases of the above-mentioned problems being discovered in various places. The telephone bureaus in various places have reported to the Ministry of Transportation to take practical measures in accordance with the city telephone business regulations, either imposing fines and making up fees, or removing the machine and suspending the call. I am afraid that telephone users in various places still have unclear situations and secretly take advantage of it, so I write it out to let them know to be vigilant and hope to correct it automatically as soon as possible to avoid being punished. In short, to seek the perfection and satisfaction of city telephone traffic, on the one hand, it depends on the telephone bureau's maintenance and proper handling, and on the other hand, the user's knowledge of following the regulations and cherishing the telephone machine is also a necessary condition. I sincerely hope that users will pay attention to it!

Trial Screening Report of Telecommunications Education Film 178

— Hua

The Film Division of the Central Party Headquarters Propaganda Committee, in order to promote the domestic production and construction undertakings, recently went to various telecommunications agencies in Shanghai to produce a telecommunications education film. It captures various machinery and work conditions of wireless telegraph and telephone, and is accompanied by audio explanations, interpreting the principles and processing procedures of various telegraph and telephone machinery, so that viewers can understand the truth of telegraph and telephone within a few tens of minutes. After the film was produced, Director Zhang of the Film Section of the Central Propaganda Committee specially invited colleagues from the Ministry of Communications to visit. The reporter happened to be present and was able to get a glimpse of the whole picture, so I will roughly describe the trial screening situation as follows:

The location of the trial screening was in the newly completed Central Photography Studio. After the reporters and others entered the studio and sat down, they heard the sound of the machine running and the screening began. The screen was unveiled, and the first thing that caught our eyes was the familiar [missing word], followed by the words "Telecommunications Construction of the Ministry of Communications" and "Filming by the Film Division of the Central Propaganda Committee", followed by various machine operations in wired telegraphy and the performance of telegraph sending and receiving procedures. The working conditions of the Morse machine, the Wheatstone machine, the Hughes machine, and the printing telegraph were all demonstrated. The reception and delivery of reports in the receiving and sending offices, such as the receipt of incoming reports, the transcription and delivery of incoming reports, etc., were all performed vividly. Among them, the use of cartoon drawings to show the movements of the air tube delivery of telegrams in the receiving and sending office, the report room, is the clearest and most moving. The accompanying audio explanation is also relevant and easy to understand, which is also valuable. The second part is the performance of wireless telegraphy. The first is the working conditions of the manual sending and receiving machine, followed by the real picture of the automatic sending and receiving machine in the central receiving and sending room of the international radio station, and then various parts such as the generator, storage battery, antenna, and ground cable of the Liuheng and Fenglinqiao receiving stations and the Zhenru transmitting station are all photographed and added with brief explanations. The third part is the performance of various telephones. The first is the method of connecting the magneto telephone, and the situation of users talking to each other. The second is the connection and call status of the common battery telephone, and the third is the performance of the automatic telephone's machinery operation and call connection. Other equipment such as storage batteries, measuring platforms, and generators in the telephone bureau are also photographed. The entire film is 2,000 feet long and takes 30 minutes to complete.

After watching the film, the reporter deeply felt that this film gave us a deeper impression than any other method. In the future, when this film is screened in major theaters, not only will the telecommunications business that the Ministry of Communications has recently been keen to innovate be directly introduced to the audience, but the general public will also be able to instill in themselves common knowledge about telecommunications. It is truly the most ideal method of social education. After the visit, I picked up my pen and wrote it down.

Air Defense Weapon 179

What Modern Publics Should Know About Telecommunications 180

— You Yu

A progressive country needs to stand on the line of the times, and the citizens of a progressive country also need to keep up with the times, because citizens are the backbone of the country. Can a country with all outdated citizens still shoulder the mission of progress? It is a necessary requirement of the new era for the telecommunications business to embark on the road of modernization and commercialization. Looking at the advanced countries in Europe and America, because of the development of science, they are all reforming and advancing towards the goals of modernization and commercialization. At the same time, their citizens have become as familiar with and use "telegraphs" as they do with "letters", and they firmly grasp the various facilities of the telegraph bureau for the convenience of public communication, and are unwilling to easily give up this right.

Looking back at the telecommunications and transportation in our country in recent years, during the period of severe national crisis, through the efforts of the transportation authorities to rectify and construct, and the thorough awakening and hard work of colleagues across the country, the practical contribution of gradually realizing the two slogans of "modernization" and "popularization" has been made. However, our sending public has always adhered to the traditional concept, and when it comes to telegrams, it seems that they must be urgent and serious matters, and they do not have a full understanding of the meaning of the above two slogans. This erroneous concept must be changed on the road to catching up with the times.

Therefore, our hope for the sending public and readers is that whenever we contribute a new set of rules or facilities, readers, please quickly study it, understand it, and use it! If there is anything that is not clear, the colleagues of the telegraph bureau or telephone bureau will sincerely answer it. For example, if you discover something in social situations, you can use social telegrams. If you want to talk to friends elsewhere, you can use long-distance calls. Or if you want to communicate with relatives and friends while sailing on a ship, you can use ship telegrams. You can also send travel telegrams to China Travel Service while traveling. Other services such as prepaid reply telegrams, follow-up telegrams, split telegrams, held telegrams, mail-forwarded telegrams, route-forwarded telegrams, and voice telegrams are all available at the sender's convenience. Now the Ministry of Communications has adopted the general method of jointly establishing postal and telecommunications offices, so telegrams or telephones can be sent or received in every place, which is even more convenient. In recent years, all kinds of reforms in telecommunications facilities have been aimed at facilitating the public. The progress of the telecommunications era is truly rapid!

In short, we hope that the public will grasp the times and deeply understand the meaning of telecommunications modernization and popularization; at the same time, we must stand on the international parallel line and catch up with the times to serve the public.

Radio Wireless in the Italo-Ethiopian War 181

— Feng

——Excerpt from the October report of the US Joint Company——

According to William A. Winterbuttom, Vice President and General Manager of the No-Money Radio Joint Company, the British Post Office's cancellation of the Italian representative's scheduled radio speech in Geneva has aroused serious attention to the complete independence of American wireless telecommunications since the war. The fully-equipped receiving stations under the organization of the Joint Company are able to listen to broadcasts from any country or other place. The broadcasts from both sides of the same event, which are related to the United States, can also be listened to. If one party is unable to broadcast directly, other countries must be prepared to broadcast for it. Last Sunday, the Italian representative, Sir Aloysius, broadcasted a radio speech directly to the American radio network from Rome, which Mr. Winterbuttom considered to be the best example. Because the London Radio Station originally scheduled to broadcast Sir Aloysius' radio speech in Geneva via the Atlantic Ocean, but the British Post Office suddenly stated that the station could not be used for the speech when the deadline arrived. Regardless of whether this was the result of technical difficulties or because the United Kingdom was a member of the League of Nations and was affected by the implementation of sanctions, the broadcast was still not prevented from being heard in the United States. Because after Sir Aloysius returned to Rome, he broadcast his delayed speech directly to the United States through his own country's radio station. The broadcast was received by the Joint Company's Riverhead Radio Station and distributed to Columbia Wireless Communications according to the scheduled method. The rebroadcast was very successful. The company has rebroadcasted the declaration of the Afghan representative in Geneva, and now, according to American broadcasting policy, it has made public the opinions of both sides of the event.

The United States has listened to the broadcasts directly from the capitals of Italy and Afghanistan, Italy and Afghanistan, and especially felt wonderful when listening to the speech of the King of Afghanistan. Because its broadcast was not only from the indigenous Di Fa Radio Station in Africa, but its machinery only used a new standard shortwave transmitter with less than five points of power.

The benefits of wireless communication are obviously significant. The telegraphic symbols reach inland towns or coastal areas with the same convenience. There are no political boundaries, and there is no need for relaying or inspection along the way. This widespread global wireless organization is not only limited to communication with foreign countries, but its great effect is far-reaching. With modern wireless communication, it is possible to transmit photos of Abyssinian military operations within 24 hours.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Amateur Anecdotes

Head in a Pile of Iron Buckets 182

— Lu Xun

A few days ago, a newspaper from another city published a piece of news about an iron bucket crushing a rickshaw driver's head, saying that a beer company wanted to move to a new location, and because they were reluctant to spend more than 20 yuan to hire a truck, someone contracted the job and hired a tiger cart (also known as a collapsing cart) to transport the goods. They stacked pairs of iron buckets full of beer on top of each other, but the iron buckets exceeded the weight that the collapsing cart could bear, causing the axle to break. The iron buckets on top rolled down and crushed the rickshaw driver's head into a "meat pie", and the brain was splashed everywhere. The rickshaw driver died on the spot. This tragic human incident is truly unbearable to witness and hear!

Because the rickshaw driver's head was crushed by the iron bucket, some people thought that the culprit should be the iron bucket, because why should the iron bucket be so heavy? Some people think that the axle of the tiger cart is too weak, and the main culprit should be the tiger cart that cannot withstand the weight. Some people even complain that the rickshaw driver himself is not good, why should he load so heavy goods, and why should he do this lowly and dangerous business? But these many people will not really recognize the main culprit of the disaster.

That's right, the rickshaw driver's head was crushed by the iron bucket, but why did the iron bucket crush the rickshaw driver's head? I think the key to the problem lies in the fact that the company wanted to save more than 20 yuan. It seems a bit strange that such a big company is reluctant to spend tens of dollars more on transportation costs, but it is not strange at all. They only know how to save costs and how to increase revenue. They have never taken the safety of workers' lives into account. In the metropolis of the foreign concessions, among the hundreds of thousands of workers who are wringing out the blood and tears of their lives, among the batches of workers who are swallowed up by the machine wheels, isn't the death of a tiger cart driver just a grain of sand in the Ganges River?

Regarding rickshaw drivers, humanitarians do not take rickshaws for the sake of humanitarianism; kind administrative authorities limit the number of rickshaw drivers for the sake of "rationalization"; their goodwill is commendable. But the former humanitarian is just an ostrich, he buries his head in the desert, thinking that he has escaped all evils "out of sight, out of mind". The latter also did not diagnose the cause of the public's life.

But the tragedy is real. Taking the life of a natural person other than oneself is called murder. Taking a step back, the responsible person of the company has committed the criminal charge of negligent homicide. The contractor who helps the evildoer and profits from it is also suspected of being an accomplice, and should be handed over to the authorities for punishment. If the law says so, this minimum mission of guaranteeing human rights can still be achieved!

The Scenery of Shanghai

Shanghai Forty-Two Years Ago 183

— Wen Zheng

——A Tour of the Old Shanghai Exhibition——

From the 26th of this month for two weeks, the people of Shanghai can have the opportunity to see the old Shanghai of forty-two years ago, because the "Old Shanghai Exhibition" is being held on the fourth floor of 55 Yuanmingyuan Road.

The people of Shanghai should remember that this year, at the Lyceum Theatre on Baoshi Road, Ms. Tang Ying, a former Shanghai celebrity, and some of her foreign friends starred in a play in Chinese ancient costumes but spoken in foreign languages. That was the English Chinese play "Wang Baochuan" also known as "Red Oriole" written by Xiong Shiyi. One of those foreigners, Mrs. Ritz, is indeed a drama fan, and can be said to be one of the people who likes Chinese art the most. She once hosted a grand tea dance party at Sassoon Garden on Hongqiao Road to welcome Dr. Mei, the king of actors who returned from Russia. The invitation she printed was very interesting. In the upper left corner of the invitation, she printed a pattern, which drew an old woman and Guan Gong's facial makeup, and had the letters IAT, which was the symbol of the "International Arts Theatre" she presided over. This lady is also one of the initiators who are most enthusiastic about supporting the "Old Shanghai Exhibition" and promoting its success.

The opening time of this exhibition is 5:15 pm on the 26th. It means to welcome the people of Shanghai to visit after office hours every day. They also invited Dr. Fei Mu, who is very familiar with the stories of Shanghai, to give a lecture. The topic of the lecture is "Shanghai Forty-Two Years Ago". The things that Dr. Fei Mu talked about are all supported by poems. After listening to his lecture, you can immediately find a lot of evidence in the exhibition, such as the paintings and photos hanging on the wall, the utensils and utensils arranged on the floor, and the large and thick books on the table.

When visitors arrive on the fourth floor, a Western lady will greet them with a smile and ask them to buy a ticket (one silver dollar). Entering the exhibition room, the first thing you see is a blackboard with some English written on it in white chalk, which is nothing more than the name of the exhibition, the exhibition period, the price of the admission ticket, and the name of the organizer. The room is neither high nor low, only the size of an ordinary theater stage. In the center, a platform was built, about one foot higher than the ground (Dr. Fei Mu stood on this platform to give lectures). A very large map was placed horizontally on the stage, and the color was already dark and there were many small damages. It was so old! Looking closely, it turned out to be a map of the Shanghai Concession 103 years ago, which was drawn by the French Concession authorities.

Next to a pillar on the front right side of the stage, a large clock was placed on a wooden frame, which was also antique. The four characters "Fulian Zen Temple" were engraved on the front, and the years of Guangxu 19th year and Xu Ruiji Foundry were engraved on one side. It is said that 35 years ago, this clock was hanging in the pagoda of the Fulian Zen Temple in Ningbo. Because the pagoda and the temple were burned down, it was transported to Shanghai. Try knocking it, the sound is very loud. According to a foreign lady who was entertaining guests next to her, "China is now preparing to manufacture a clock that is more than ten times larger than this. Is this the only metal casting art that the Chinese regard as?" The reporter was ashamed to be an amateur and dared not answer. However, there are many devout men and women who are working hard to promote the Heavenly Clock of Jiuhua Mountain. Moreover, it seems that in fact, the Buddhist practice of wasting people and money is also praised as a magnificent achievement of ancient art! So, the foreign lady understands art!

Next to another pillar on the front left side of the stage, there is a wardrobe, which is completely vermilion lacquer, about eight feet high. The red lacquer color is bright and clean, which is indeed a representative work of China. Next to the wardrobe is a long incense table, which is the kind of large and long incense table that used to be placed in front of the screen door in the main hall of old-fashioned Shanghai families. By custom, most of them put a large self-ringing clock in the middle, an antique porcelain vase on the side, and a marble screen on the right. In front of the incense table are an eight-immortal table, two master chairs, and so on. There are photos on the incense table, which are some of the landscapes of Shanghai's changes in the past 50 years. On the wall opposite the incense table are two spring benches, with the same dark lacquer as the incense table, and the light can illuminate people. The walls of the spring bench display are full of old Shanghai maps, but they are limited to the concessions. From 103 years ago to 53 years ago, there are hanging pictures, and from 50 years ago, there have been many photos. According to the reporter's speculation, the things from 42 years ago and later are better in the system, and it can be seen that special attention has been paid to the collection of these materials since 42 years ago!

According to the elders, Shanghai forty-two years ago did not have electric lights at that time, only gas lights, that is, gas lamps. There were already paddle steamers and small steamers towing civilian ships from Shanghai to Suzhou. The famous Four Horse Road in Shanghai at that time had five-story buildings, teahouses such as Qingliang Pavilion and Chuixiao Pin Yu Lou. Opium smoking was sold openly; the five-story building and Qingliang Pavilion were divided into front and back halls, with tea seats in the front hall and smoke shops (with pit-beds and tables) in the back hall. At that time, foreigners were not as pretentious as they are now, but Cantonese and Ningbo people were more pretentious. In the Old Shanghai Exhibition, there is a record book of Jardine Matheson, in which you can still find the foreigners' petitions to the Chinese government, in which they call themselves Yi Min and call the Chinese government officials adults. This was the situation before the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895, and after the Sino-Japanese War (forty years from today), it went from bad to worse.

In the Jardine Matheson record book of the exhibition, there is a notice-like thing posted as follows. You can see how pretentious the foreign businessmen were. The notice was written by Jardine, the consul of the Yellow Flag stationed in Guangdong: To the effect that the name of the boatman in Huangpu, Sansheng (a contractor), is accompanied by 40 sailors, who are going to ×× to wait for the news of the British steamer's monthly letter, and rushing to the province. I hope that the patrol boat along the way will open the letter and check it before letting it go, and do not delay it for a long time, lest it delay the company. This is a real letter of credence. According to its English explanation, it was written by the Danish consul in Guangdong for Jardine Matheson. A certificate from a foreign consul can pass through the Chinese Kexun patrol boat. This was already commonplace in the 28th year of Daoguang. Next to the Jardine Matheson record book is full of photos, which fully show the changes in uniforms in Shanghai from more than 50 years ago to the present. There are uniform styles for the army (limited to the jurisdiction of the Public Works Bureau), staff, and many other employees. There are also many portraits of farmers, workers, merchants, and farmers in the streets and alleys. Although it feels a bit messy, you can also see a lot of the scenery of old Shanghai there.

In the eyes of those foreign ladies who are in charge of this exhibition, the nature of this exhibition is mostly seen from the perspective of novelty and antiques; but in the eyes of us Shanghai people, it is not difficult to find many traces of turning from masters to slaves. I think that all Shanghai people should pay attention to this point, and in the future, Shanghai people should prepare for the exhibition themselves.

Industry Survey

The "Used Leather Shoes" Industry in Harbin 184

— Lu Ren

In Harbin, there are many unique industries that surprise newcomers. Take the selling of used leather shoes, for example. This small-scale business wouldn't be an industry anywhere else, but here it holds a significant commercial position, even though their business locations aren't formal shops.

This business of selling used leather shoes is commonly known here as the "black business." They gather in both Daoli and Daowai districts. During the time when the Russians held power here, their business was very prosperous. Now, because most of the residents here don't need to wear leather shoes, they only rely on a portion of Chinese people and passing merchants to patronize their business.

The reason why selling used leather shoes is called "black business" is that their business hours are entirely at night, and the locations where they gather are chosen next to dimly lit roads, so that customers, even with their best vision, can't discern any flaws on the leather shoes, because only in this way can transactions be easily successful.

It is said that Harbin used to have more than 500 places involved in this used leather shoe industry, directly or indirectly supporting at least ten to twenty thousand people. Now, because business is slow, only about three hundred shoe stalls remain. However, compared to other cities, the number is probably still considerable. Every night at dusk, no matter which road you step on, you can see a few dimly lit shoe stalls. A piece of blue cloth, about ten feet square, displays rows and rows of leather shoes. The leather shoes are shiny and lustrous, and at first glance, they look even more attractive than new leather shoes in a shoe store. Because they excessively embellish those old leather shoes, passersby are often drawn to admire them for a while. If someone hasn't lived in Harbin for long and sees this kind of "cheap and good" (?) merchandise, they will inevitably be driven by greed to buy them.

As for the styles of leather shoes on these used leather shoe stalls, probably even a decent shoe store can't match their variety. They have women's new-style high-heeled shoes, flat shoes, the most popular cut-out floral shoes, children's strap shoes, high-soled shoes, men's pointed-toe shoes, round-toe shoes, American-style leather shoes, Russian-style leather shoes, military riding boots... all kinds of men's and women's leather shoes are available. The source of these used leather shoes is quite thought-provoking. The main source, of course, is "second-hand" from those who "collect junk." The next source is being intertwined with the stolen goods market. Buying and selling used leather shoes, this in and out, although connected, are operated independently. Buying used leather shoes is done by "junk collectors." In addition to buying newspapers, glass bottles, broken clothes, sundries, etc., what they welcome most are used leather shoes. After the used leather shoes are collected, they are carried to the "junk market" and resold to leather shoe repairmen. In this transfer process, "junk collectors" earn at most only one or two dimes per pair. The ones who enjoy high profits are those shoemakers with repair skills and leather shoe "dealers" with sufficient capital. In addition, stolen goods from petty thieves are directly purchased by leather shoe "dealers," and "junk collectors" are not allowed to intervene. Because most leather shoe "dealers" have some hidden power, most thieves need to rely on their protection. However, in this industry, there are also so-called "trusts" and other business organizations. A "trust" leader must possess both financial and human resources. They must have a large amount of capital to buy goods that others dare not buy, and they must also have the power to "pull strings" for any "mishaps" that occur when buying goods. With this power, they can simultaneously operate buying, repairing, and selling. However, very few people in the used leather shoe industry have this ability. Most of the others only do repair work and don't also sell. Those who sell are not good at repairing. At most, they are repairmen during the day and become the owners of used leather shoes at night.

The usual value of a pair of used leather shoes is at most only thirty cents when buying, but after being resold by the "junk collector," it will be sold for about fifty or sixty cents. After going through the hands of repairmen and leather shoe "dealers," the price increases to two yuan and several dimes. Although this profit is very high, buyers don't feel it's expensive. Because in Harbin, buying a pair of high-quality leather shoes costs more than ten yuan, and even a slightly inferior pair costs seven or eight yuan. Compared to a pair of used leather shoes for more than two yuan, the latter is certainly cheaper. Moreover, the cost of nailing the front and back soles of a pair of leather shoes usually costs one yuan and seventy or eighty cents! Therefore, the petty bourgeoisie with limited financial means are still happy to be customers of those used shoe stalls.

The capital of a shoe stall varies greatly. The largest ones have three to five hundred yuan, while the smallest ones have only over a hundred yuan. The owners of these stalls are sometimes people who made money from "collecting junk" and changed careers to sell used leather shoes. Some are unemployed shoe workers who, without formal work, pool some money to start their own "business." Large shoe stalls sometimes don't have enough capital on their own, so they gather three to five people to operate in partnership. Small stalls are mostly operated independently. However, why are some people willing to partner to run a large stall instead of operating independently? There is a "big fish eats small fish" effect. Because shoe stalls with large capital can absorb goods from all sides, such as pointed-toe, wide-toe, round-toe, slightly convex, square, as well as Russian-style, Japanese-style, and local styles, they can accommodate all kinds of different customers to choose from, and the business will naturally be more prosperous. However, shoe stalls with small capital dare not absorb these kinds of goods in large quantities. Most of what they have are some common styles, so they can only accommodate fewer customers. In addition, large shoe stalls have lower interest because their business is prosperous. But small shoe stalls cannot do this because they don't have many shoe styles, and it's hard to expect a few customers to visit in a day. If they sell too cheaply, there's not much profit. Therefore, small shoe stalls generally don't want to be neighbors with large shoe stalls, but because they cannot withstand the pressure of capital.

Current Affairs Research

The Restoration Movements in Greece and Austria 185

— Xi Ren

Recently, two European countries have experienced restoration movements: Greece, one of the important countries in the Balkan Peninsula, and Austria, a country known for its troubles. Now, the restoration movement in Greece has been successful. King George II has already returned to Athens and will soon exercise his royal power, commissioning the formation of a new government. As for the restoration movement in Austria, it is currently underway and is quite intense. Whether it can achieve victory like Greece is still a big question. However, the success of the restoration movement in Greece and the ongoing restoration movement in Austria are not only problems for these two countries but also have a significant impact on the overall situation in Europe. Therefore, we will discuss both of them together here.

First, let's talk about the restoration in Greece. On the surface, the re-emergence of imperial politics in Greece seems to be entirely the result of the national referendum held in November. In fact, the struggle between the monarchists and republicans in Greece has a long history and complex international relations.

Greece is a semi-colonial country, and all its internal events are deeply related to the European powers. We can easily understand the significance of the Greek monarchists' great victory if we simply look at the fact that the Greek restoration movement occurred at the very moment when the United Kingdom and Italy were in sharp opposition in the Mediterranean. Geographically, Greece is bordered by the Aegean Sea to the east, the Mediterranean Sea to the south, and the Ionian Sea to the west. Its coastline is the longest in the world, and it has many bays and islands, most of which are very important. It is a country valued by European powers, especially the United Kingdom and Italy, in their competition in the Mediterranean and the Balkans. If Italy were to acquire Greece and use its geographical advantages, it would be possible to seize Malta, the United Kingdom's base in the Mediterranean, at any time and further drive the British out of the Mediterranean. Conversely, the United Kingdom must obtain the active assistance of Greece to contend with Italy in the Mediterranean. Therefore, the United Kingdom and Italy have always been secretly competing for Greece, and the Greek royalists have developed under the support of the United Kingdom. Recently, due to the outbreak of the Italian-Ethiopian War, the conflict between the United Kingdom and Italy in the Mediterranean has become even more acute and realistic. In order to actively use Greece to contain Italy, the British took advantage of Italy's involvement in East Africa to encourage the Greek royalists to announce the abandonment of the republic and implement the monarchy as soon as possible. Originally, the implementation of the monarchy in Greece was to be decided by a referendum last month, but Greek Army Chief and royalist leader Kondylis, fearing that the opportunity would be missed, instigated the military on October 10 to force the Tsaldaris cabinet to resign. The National Assembly then announced the abolition of the republic and welcomed George II back to the throne. Kondylis appointed himself regent and temporarily formed an interim transitional cabinet. As a result, the November referendum was held under the manipulation of the royalists. The results showed that 1,527,712 people participated in the vote, of which 1,491,992 voted in favor of the monarchy, 32,454 voted in favor of the republic, and 3,268 votes were invalid. The monarchists won an overwhelming victory with a majority of 90%. However, this victory of the Greek monarchists was also a victory for the United Kingdom in Greece.

Of course, the realization of the Greek restoration has not only external relations but also internal causes. In fact, after five or six years of economic panic, the poverty of the countryside, the decline of the cities, the increase in unemployment, and the increasingly painful lives of the general public have made it impossible for this small country to maintain a peaceful state. Extraordinary phenomena such as so-called political strikes have become commonplace in Greece in the past few months. Obviously, it was the military coup led by Greek Liberal Party leader Venizelos in March of this year, which involved a part of the army and navy, that caused the Greek civil war that shook Europe. Although this was a military coup on the surface, a large number of people participated in the event, making it a popular movement in Greece on the other hand. In this situation, the tendency of the two extremes of Greek politics has become an obvious fact. In order to attack the republicans and suppress the people, the monarchists, with the support of the United Kingdom, seized the opportunity to implement the restoration in advance and abolish the republican system.

Originally, since the Greek monarchists won the election in 1933, the power of the monarchists has been secretly expanding after Tsaldaris, the leader of the People's Party close to the monarchy, formed a cabinet. After the Venizelos coup in March of this year was suppressed, the power of the Greek republicans was greatly hit, and royalist leader Kondylis seized control of the Greek government by putting down the internal unrest. Afterwards, the monarchists continued to attack the republicans and gradually launched a restoration movement. But at this time, the republicans still had considerable power, and few of the general public supported the restoration, so after the cabinet reshuffle in July, the royalists still did not dare to openly advocate for the restoration. Recently, after the royalists had made sufficient preparations, they took advantage of the conflict between the United Kingdom and Italy to carry out a restoration coup in advance without waiting for a referendum. They abolished the republic and realized the monarchy in one fell swoop. This is the recent history of the Greek restoration.

Now, George II has returned to Athens, and the fact that Greece has changed from a republic to a monarchy has become a reality. There is certainly no question about that. But whether the volatile Greece can be stable in the future is still a question. First of all, the restoration in Greece is naturally supported by the United Kingdom. Even France, because of its relationship with the Little Entente and Kondylis, and in order to deal with Italy in the Mediterranean, does not oppose it. However, Italy is not very happy about the restoration in Greece. Although George II passed through Rome and met with the Italian King and Mussolini when he returned to his country, Italy still does not want the royalists to hold power in Greece in its heart. Now, Mussolini is focusing on East Africa and certainly has no time to take care of the Balkans or Greece, but who can say that Italy will not continue to operate in Greece in the future? Secondly, the realization of the Greek restoration has not solved the fundamental problems of the domestic economy and politics, and the power of the Republicans has not been completely lost. In the future, anti-monarchical movements may continue to occur in Greece. Therefore, although the Greek royalists and the United Kingdom behind them have won a temporary victory, Greece and even Europe will still not be stable in the future.

The second is the ongoing restoration movement in Austria. Originally, the restoration movement in Austria had a long history, but it had not been realized in the past because the Austrian-Hungarian problem was too complex and serious. Recently, at a time when Europe is troubled, the restoration movement in Austria has become more intense, and Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg and Vice-Chancellor Prince Starhemberg have also participated in restoration demonstrations. Therefore, the Austrian problem has once again become one of the important issues that European countries are paying attention to.

The complexity and importance of the Austrian problem have been discussed too much in other publications, and we do not want to explain it in detail here. What we want to say now is only the current restoration movement in Austria. The mastermind behind this movement is undoubtedly Italy. Because once the Austrian restoration is realized, it will inevitably affect Hungary, and as a result, Austria-Hungary will become attached to Italy, and Italy will dominate Central Europe and become the leader of the Danube. According to Havas, because "a noble of the old Habsburg royal family of Austria has formed a marital alliance with a princess of Italy," Italy does not resolutely oppose the restoration in Austria. This is certainly a formalistic view. However, from the fundamental interests of Italy and Austria, Italy not only does not oppose the restoration in Austria but also wants it to be realized as soon as possible.

However, France's satellite Little Entente will feel a headache when they hear that Austria is going to be restored. Because if the Austrian restoration is realized, Hungary will be affected, and as a result, Austria-Hungary will merge, cutting the Little Entente in the middle and preventing them from contacting each other. At the same time, Hitler, who is plotting the annexation of Austria and Germany, certainly does not want Austria to be restored. Therefore, after the news of the development of the restoration movement in Austria spread, the Little Entente, France, and Germany all expressed their firm opposition. Although the United Kingdom has not yet expressed its attitude, it can be expected that it will not support the restoration in Austria when it is trying to change the nature of the imperialist Second World War by solving the Austrian problem. In this situation, we can say that the restoration movement in Austria will never be as smooth as that in Greece, and its victory is unlikely in the near future.

In short, the realization of the restoration in Greece and the development of the restoration movement in Austria are both manifestations of the contradictions of the European powers. This is not surprising in troubled Europe.

Common Knowledge

The Suez Canal 186

— Ji Liang

Since the outbreak of the Italian-Ethiopian War, there have been rumors that the League of Nations would blockade the Suez Canal. For a time, the name "Suez Canal" was almost more valued than the Mediterranean. Because the Suez Canal is geographically located on the Isthmus of Suez in Egypt, connecting the Red Sea and the Mediterranean Sea, it is a vital transportation route. With it, the three continents of Europe, Asia, and Africa are connected. If the Suez Canal is really blockaded, it will be very difficult for Italian troops to be transported to East Africa. As a result, not only will the situation of the Italian-Ethiopian War change, but the Italian colonies in East Africa may also have problems. Therefore, if the United Kingdom were to blockade the Suez Canal, Italy would very likely resist by force, which would result in the faster outbreak of the Second World War. This is why people are paying special attention to the Suez Canal at this time.

Speaking of the history of the Suez Canal, we can easily think of the division of Africa by the European powers in the 19th century. Around 1850, apart from Egypt, an ancient civilized country in Africa, the other parts of Africa were still unknown to the world. Later, due to the urgent demand for colonies by the European powers, many explorers went deep into the interior of Africa to explore. Then merchants and politicians came to this "dark and mysterious continent." Then people knew that Africa also has huge inland seas, magnificent rivers and waterfalls, exotic fruits, flowers, plants and insects, great and beautiful forests and mountains, strange and terrifying wild beasts, and abundant products. For the convenience of colonizing Africa and for the convenience of invading Asia, countries such as the United Kingdom and France implemented the construction of the Suez Canal. The construction was presided over by the Frenchman Lesseps. It took ten years from 1859 to 1861 to complete, costing 200 million yuan, with a total length of 87 miles. Because of this canal, Europeans not only easily colonized Africa but also more easily invaded Asia. For example, the United Kingdom in India, Burma, the Malay Islands, France in Indochina, the Netherlands in the Malay Archipelago, Italy in East Africa, and the United Kingdom, France, Spain, Portugal, and Belgium in Africa all relied on the Suez Canal as a transportation line to carry out their invasions. Therefore, the European powers paid great attention to Su

The following is continued on page 5.

Page 22

Page 23

ez Canal and have signed strict treaties to protect the safety of the canal.

The Suez Canal is operated by the Suez Canal Universal Company, which obtained a 99-year right of use from the Egyptian government. The company has a total of 800,000 shares, of which more than 353,000 are in the hands of the British government. The reason why the United Kingdom holds so many shares is that it bought 176,600 shares from Egypt in 1875. In addition to the United Kingdom, the remaining shares are scattered among the French people. However, the Canal Company does not have absolute political authority. Because the canal is still a part of Egyptian territory, and the Canal Company has confirmed that the Egyptian government has the right to protect and police the canal without prejudice to the freedom of navigation.

In October 1888, representatives of the United Kingdom, France, Russia, Germany, Austria-Hungary, Turkey, Italy, Spain, the Netherlands, and Egypt held a conference in Constantinople and concluded a treaty stipulating the neutrality of the Suez Canal. The main points of the treaty are as follows:

1. The Suez Canal shall be free to navigate in wartime or peacetime, regardless of the nationality of the ship.

2. Belligerent acts are prohibited within three miles of the canal and its mouth.

3. When warships of belligerent countries pass through the canal, they are not allowed to stay in the port of Suez for more than 24 hours unless they encounter irresistible events such as natural disasters.

4. After the warships of the belligerent countries pass, the warships of the opposing party cannot depart until 24 hours have passed.

5. The Turkish Emperor and the Egyptian King have police power over the Suez Canal.

Therefore, the powers are not allowed to act arbitrarily on the Suez Canal. For example, during the Russo-Japanese War, although Japan was an ally of the United Kingdom at the time, the British had to acquiesce to the passage of Russian warships through the Suez Canal to attack Japan. Again, during the Italian-Turkish War in 1911, although Egypt was the territory of Turkey, it could not prevent the Italian navy from freely traveling in the canal. From this, we can see the attitude of the powers towards the Suez Canal.

However, when the so-called emergency really comes, the powers will not abide by the treaty. In fact, although the Suez Canal has the above provisions and there have been facts of compliance with the provisions in the past, there have still been three blockades. First, when the Egyptian revolution against the Egyptian Governor occurred, the British army seized the canal for three days and prohibited ships from passing through. Second, when Spain and the United Kingdom were at war in 1898, the canal authorities prohibited the Spanish fleet from loading coal while navigating the canal. Third, during the Great War in Europe, the canal was temporarily blocked due to the entry and exit of Turkish warships. Naturally, except for these short periods, the canal maintained a normal state of free navigation during the long-term war.

In 1919, although the Paris Peace Conference decided that Egypt was a British protectorate, the United Kingdom obtained the right to protect the Suez Canal at the Paris Peace Conference. When it recognized the independence of Egypt in 1922, it still declared that it would retain this right. Egypt has never recognized this statement by the United Kingdom, it is only a unilateral statement by the United Kingdom. But therefore, everything in Egypt is still subject to British control. When the United Kingdom and Egypt signed a treaty in 1929, the United Kingdom made a further expression on the independence of Egypt on the surface, but it still used the pretext of protecting the Suez Canal to station considerable troops in Egypt and still interfered in Egypt's internal affairs in practice.

Because the United Kingdom can control Egypt, obtain the right to protect the Suez Canal, and hold a majority of the shares, the actual power of the canal is now mostly in the hands of the British. At present, Italy's expedition to East Africa is threatening British interests, but the British have not resolutely blockaded the Suez Canal to trouble Italy because they are afraid of the international situation and dare not act arbitrarily.

Now, the Egyptian independence movement is developing, and the atmosphere of war in East Africa continues to rise, and the results will have a great impact on the situation in the Suez Canal. Let's watch.

Literary Works

Recovering the Account Book (5) 187

— Pu Yu

"Of course. My relationship helped the other day, but if you weren't greedy for a bargain, it wouldn't have become a reality. You only paid 400 yuan in tax for over 200 *dan* of wine (equivalent to over 20,000 *jin* by pound measurement). To be honest, I was considerate of the merchants' situation and didn't want you to pay more. What good did I get out of it myself?..."

"It's not my fault, if... if it goes to the provincial bureau, it's not... it's not me personally who suffers!"

Damn it, you can't judge a book by its cover; he even has the audacity to appeal! I was just preparing to attack him again, but luckily old Jiang stepped up for me:

"Boss Li, you have no grounds for defense. You say you paid taxes, do you have any evidence? Did the director give you a receipt for the money? Relying solely on verbal statements in official matters will subject you to punishment for slandering public officials! Not to mention, our director was originally kind-hearted, who knew you would offend others and get secretly reported. This time, the provincial bureau's official matter is solely focused on your tax evasion, and we only have the responsibility to handle it."

The old man's face turned increasingly green, his throat swelled up, and his hands kept clenching and unclenching. I could see the anger, resentment, sadness, and anxiety in his heart; he was also preparing methods of struggle. Finally, he suddenly became excited and said resolutely:

"Fine! I only blame myself for opening a brewery, I'm just giving money away and accompanying you to a lawsuit!"

At this moment, I was annoyed and anxious, feeling that the old man had turned into a stubborn wild beast; not listening to my command, not restrained by me. But perhaps it was a last flash of defiance, and I would ultimately deliver him a fatal blow.

"Damn it, a lawsuit? The common people going against public officials is just asking for trouble!" I cursed in my heart. Indeed, if the old man really overestimated himself and wanted to oppose me, then don't blame me for being unscrupulous; I would immediately report him to the provincial bureau with an official document, falsely accusing him of tax evasion, and find a few people to testify. Where would he go to argue? But then again, I didn't want to cause trouble either, as long as the old man could stay within my control. So I deliberately put on a peaceful face and softened my voice:

"Boss Li, I, Liu, am a good friend! The other day, I collected less tax from you out of consideration, and today, it's for official matters - but I didn't use any official pretense, I'm speaking entirely out of personal friendship, but you insist on putting on a stern face and accompanying me to a lawsuit..." I paused for two minutes, watching his expression, "Have you decided?" Seeing that he still showed a stubborn unwillingness to yield, I felt that I had to crush his resistance: "Fine! Then I'll have to be rude!"

So I ordered Jiang Xiwu to open his briefcase and take out the ultimate weapon: the red list and seals. The old man's overly frightened eyes were fixed on Jiang Xiwu's movements. I took the red list and read it to him very sternly: (To be continued)

Movie News

Shakespeare's "A Midsummer Night's Dream" 189

Finally Realized on the Screen

When "A Midsummer Night's Dream" A Midsummer Nigit Dream opens, if ghosts have souls, Shakespeare would definitely be amazed by the scenes projected on the screen! For someone who lived in an era when stage backgrounds and photography techniques had not yet been invented, just seeing actors active on a stage with gorgeous forest and splendid palace backgrounds would already seem like watching magic. Now, wouldn't these novel film techniques be even more astonishing to him?

This fantasy story has been performed countless times on stages around the world. In the earliest days, it was on a simple and innocent stage, without backgrounds, and the scenes in the play had to be imagined by the audience themselves. Later, stage backgrounds were invented, but even the largest stages and the best designs are ultimately overshadowed by Reinhardt's screen version of "A Midsummer Night's Dream."

You see, in this film, the forest seems to have no end, unlike the stage where there is a backdrop to limit it. There are also a hundred fairies dancing in the moonlight; human heads are exchanged with donkey heads; Oberon brings his many large bats into the forest, looking like real bats. All of this can only be achieved with film technology.

In short, Warner Brothers, after more than two years of time, spending 1.5 million gold yuan, and exhausting the efforts of thousands of people, actually realized Shakespeare's dream on the screen. The film will soon be shown at the Guotai Cinema. If you want to experience the dreamlike scenes in the film, please wait and see.

Xu Lai in "Boatman's Daughter" 190

Su Shi said, "It is a pity that Jia Yi was the assistant of a king, but he could not use his talent himself."

Every time I think of these words, I feel deeply moved. I don't believe that anyone is absolutely without talent, even the most ordinary person must have their use. The question is how to discover their talent, how to develop their talent. As long as they can be used according to their ability, it is not difficult to achieve amazing results.

People often say, "Xu Lai is not good at acting." But who can still make such a cold assessment of Xu Lai in "Boatman's Daughter"? When she was a model, she originally wanted to cry, but the young masters insisted that she smile; her expression and movements at that time still seem to be before my eyes. The scene in the brothel upstairs and the final reunion of father and daughter are both worthy of the audience's praise.

How did Xu Lai suddenly achieve such success in "Boatman's Daughter"? I believe that this must be attributed to the director, Mr. Lu Xiling. Whether an actor can succeed is certainly related to their own talent, but if there is no director to discover their talent and develop their talent, even with extraordinary abilities, I am afraid there is a risk of being buried.
